## Page 5

Add On Services Descriptions:


Remote Op ForensicsRemoteOps Forensics is a digital forensics and incident response solution that automates
forensic evidence collection and speeds up deep investigations. It offers customized data
collection to reduce complexity and costs.


Threat Detection for NetappAn AI-powered cloud data security solution that protects NetApp arrays from malware. It offers
high-performance, low-latency inline scans that provide verdicts in milliseconds, ensuring
seamless protection without impacting performance


Cloud Funnel Data ExportA required license for exporting EDR data from the Platform to be ingested into other sources
like S3, Azure, and other MDR services like Secureworks.


SentinelOne UniversityOne year of access for one user to the online training platform. Includes videos, articles, live
training, and self paced courses.


WatchTower Pro24/7/365 threat hunting service that continuously scans customers' environments for new known
threats and IoCs. Includes access to a threat advisor to do custom hunts.


PurpleAIGenerate AI LLM that can search and analyze EDR and SDL data to find threats, summarize
findings, create searches, and answer questions about the environment or support needs.


Threat IntelligenceAn external threat feed that includes threat actors’ motives, targets, and attack behaviors to help
make informed decisions about protection from future threats and detecting IoCs and enrich
incident-related context.


Cloud Native Security Foundations Agentless (CNAPP) that secures cloud infrastructure. It includes an Offensive Security Engine
to identify exploitable vulnerabilities, a Secrets Scanning Engine for detecting hardcoded
secrets, and fix cloud misconfigurations.


Cloud Native Security ProUpgrading to Cloud Native Security Pro adds Cloud Detection and Response, Singularity Data
Lake integration, and auto-remediation with integrations with webhooks.


Mobile Guided OnboardingA 3 month engagement with an onboarding specialist who develops a deployment plan, meets
regularly with customers, and answers questions about the Mobile Threat Defense solution
during an implementation.


Guided OnboardingA 3 month engagement with an onboarding specialist who develops a deployment plan, meets
regularly with customers, and answers questions about any of the products from SentinelOne
(excluding Mobile) being implemented.


WatchTower Pro

43230000-24-STC
Digital Security Solutions

Solution Proposed: Armis: Centrix Asset Management*_


*Armis for Asset Management consolidates asset data into one complete, de-duplicated and authoritative
asset map. Creates a complete asset inventory of all asset types from the ground to the cloud ensuring
the entire attack surface is both defended and managed in real time. Complete visibility into assets
behaviors and risk management based on business context, threat and vulnerability insights and the
collective intelligence of billions of assets monitored by the Armis Asset Intelligence Engine. Asset
minimum 2000 per tenant. Network ports also known as collectors.

## **Additional Okta Solutions**

**Identity Governance**
Okta Identity Governance streamlines user access oversight by automating reviews,
certifications, and approval processes. It ensures compliance with regulations and reduces risks
by giving organizations full visibility and control over access policies.


**Workflow**
Okta Workflow is a no-code automation platform that connects identity events to IT and
business processes. It enables organizations to create custom workflows for user provisioning,
deprovisioning, and notifications without writing code, enhancing efficiency and reducing errors.


**Lifecycle Management (LCM)**
Okta LCM automates the onboarding and offboarding of users across all systems, ensuring the
right access is provisioned or revoked. It integrates seamlessly with HR systems, reducing
manual efforts and improving security.


43230000-24-STC
Digital Security Solutions




---

## Page 171

**Device Access**
Okta Device Access secures access to enterprise resources by enforcing policies on enrolled
devices. It ensures only trusted devices can access sensitive data, bolstering endpoint security
in zero-trust environments.


**Access Gateway**
Okta Access Gateway extends modern identity capabilities to on-premise applications. It
integrates legacy systems with Okta's cloud-based authentication, enabling a hybrid approach
to identity management.


**Identity Threat Protection (ITP)**
Okta ITP safeguards against identity-based attacks by detecting and mitigating threats like
phishing and credential stuffing. It leverages contextual signals, adaptive policies, and advanced
threat intelligence.


**Identity Security Posture Management (ISPM)**
Okta ISPM provides continuous monitoring and assessment of identity configurations. It
identifies and addresses vulnerabilities to maintain a secure identity environment and align with
zero-trust principles.


43230000-24-STC
Digital Security Solutions

gigabytes or terabytes, and operates on a subscription basis with annual or multi-year
commitments. Splunk Cloud can only be purchased by increments of 50GB, with 50GB being
the minimum. Pricing below is not to exceed pricing for Splunk Cloud w/ encryption at rest.

(HIPPA/PCI). In addition to Splunk Cloud, Splunk can also be deployed on-prem.

## Page 337

**Professional services -** are billed on a per-day basis. Splunk PS has created Implementation
Packages aligned to our products. Depending on the scope of a customer's license and

environment, the amount of professional services required will vary. Cost for professional
services will be billed as they are used. Each customer will be scoped according to their
products, data sources, data size, users, dashboards, reports and SOAR playbooks. These
services will be delivered remotely. If the customer requires on-site resources, travel and
expense costs will be incurred.


**Training Units -** also known as "education credits" or "training credits", are Splunk Educationspecific currency that can be used on any paid Splunk training offering.

## Page 371

# **Attachment B** **Price Proposal**

Respondent shall provide a Price Proposal for each Solution proposed for a given Service
Category. Pricing proposed shall be used by the Department to evaluate the Respondent’s
Solution. Provide Price Proposals in a PDF file. **Provision of a Price Proposal is a mandatory**
**responsiveness requirement** .


**Mandatory Requirements** . On each Price Proposal submitted, Respondent shall, at a
minimum: (1) state the applicable Service Category, (2) provide the name of the Solution
proposed, and (3) provide pricing information for the proposed Solution for both the initial and
renewal term. If no renewal pricing is proposed, Respondent affirms its submitted pricing for the
initial term shall be applicable to any renewal terms.


The Department prefers that Respondent’s pricing:


1) Provides not-to-exceed pricing for initial term and renewal term of the Solution; and

2) Provides Tiered Pricing, where greater numbers of units purchased provide
discounted pricing.


Provision of not-to-exceed pricing and tiered pricing is not a mandatory requirement, but will
result in the Respondent receiving a higher Price Proposal score, as further explained in
Attachment C, Evaluation Criteria.


Add-On Services ( **OPTIONAL** ): Respondent may include the names, descriptions, and prices
for Add-On services for the proposed Solution in its Price Proposal. If the Solution has separate
charges for implementation, integration, or other start-up costs, these must be included in the
Add-On Services portion of the Respondent’s Price Proposal. For each Add-On Service
proposed, Respondent shall describe the Add-On Service. Descriptions for each Add-On
Service should be a maximum of 250 words. Failure to enter a name, description, and price for
each proposed Add-On Service may result in that Add-On Service not being made available on
the Term Contract, if awarded. If the Renewal Term Add-On Services is not provided,
Respondent affirms pricing for the Initial Term shall be applicable to any renewal terms.


The Department reserves the right to seek clarification where necessary regarding all submitted
Price Proposals.


A sample Price Proposal is provided on the following page. Respondents are encouraged to
utilize the sample to ensure that the requirements specified above are provided, but may utilize
an alternative format that contains the required information.

**Professional services -** are billed on a per-day basis. Splunk PS has created Implementation

environment, the amount of professional services required will vary. Cost for professional

services will be billed as they are used. Each customer will be scoped according to their

services will be delivered remotely. If the customer requires on-site resources, travel and
expense costs will be incurred.

## Page 409

# **Attachment B** **Price Proposal**

Respondent shall provide a Price Proposal for each Solution proposed for a given Service
Category. Pricing proposed shall be used by the Department to evaluate the Respondent’s
Solution. Provide Price Proposals in a PDF file. **Provision of a Price Proposal is a mandatory**
**responsiveness requirement** .


**Mandatory Requirements** . On each Price Proposal submitted, Respondent shall, at a
minimum: (1) state the applicable Service Category, (2) provide the name of the Solution
proposed, and (3) provide pricing information for the proposed Solution for both the initial and
renewal term. If no renewal pricing is proposed, Respondent affirms its submitted pricing for the
initial term shall be applicable to any renewal terms.


The Department prefers that Respondent’s pricing:


1) Provides not-to-exceed pricing for initial term and renewal term of the Solution; and

2) Provides Tiered Pricing, where greater numbers of units purchased provide
discounted pricing.


Provision of not-to-exceed pricing and tiered pricing is not a mandatory requirement, but will
result in the Respondent receiving a higher Price Proposal score, as further explained in
Attachment C, Evaluation Criteria.


Add-On Services ( **OPTIONAL** ): Respondent may include the names, descriptions, and prices
for Add-On services for the proposed Solution in its Price Proposal. If the Solution has separate
charges for implementation, integration, or other start-up costs, these must be included in the
Add-On Services portion of the Respondent’s Price Proposal. For each Add-On Service
proposed, Respondent shall describe the Add-On Service. Descriptions for each Add-On
Service should be a maximum of 250 words. Failure to enter a name, description, and price for
each proposed Add-On Service may result in that Add-On Service not being made available on
the Term Contract, if awarded. If the Renewal Term Add-On Services is not provided,
Respondent affirms pricing for the Initial Term shall be applicable to any renewal terms.


The Department reserves the right to seek clarification where necessary regarding all submitted
Price Proposals.


A sample Price Proposal is provided on the following page. Respondents are encouraged to
utilize the sample to ensure that the requirements specified above are provided, but may utilize
an alternative format that contains the required information.


43230000-24-STC Page of **1** **18**
Digital Security Solutions
